Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\n\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \"Create login form\" not \"Build entire auth system\")\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\n\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\n- Easier to track progress\n- Can resume if interrupted\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\n- Parallel work possible in future\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\n1. User says: \"I want a web app with login and dashboard\"\n2. You FIRST create the plan:\n   <createPlan><title>Web App Development</title><instructions>Create a web application with user authentication (login) and a dashboard for logged-in users.</instructions></createPlan>\n3. Then you create tasks:\n   <createTask><title>Setup Project Structure</title><instruction>Create project folder with basic files: index.html, style.css, app.js, server.py. Add login endpoint /api/login that validates username/password and returns JWT token. Add /api/dashboard endpoint that requires auth.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Frontend Login</title><instruction>Create index.html with login form. Connect to /api/login. Store JWT token in localStorage. Redirect to dashboard on success.</instruction></createTask>\n   <createTask><title>Build Dashboard</title><instruction>Create dashboard view. Fetch user data from /api/dashboard with token. Display user info and logout button.</instruction></createTask>\n\nWhen all tasks are created, tell the user \"Plan is ready! <!-- {"role": "system", "content": "\nYou are in BUILD MODE. You are code agent. Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.\n\nMODE: BUILD (Thinking ENABLED - you can reason step by step)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n1. You will receive tasks automatically (from plan mode). Execute each task using available tools.\n2. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.\n3. MANDATORY PROGRESS REPORTING: After completing any meaningful step, call <LogProgress><taskId>TASK_ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Specific action completed</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n4. MANDATORY SELF-VERIFICATION: Before calling <nextTask>completed</nextTask>, verify your work:\n   - If you wrote code: verify it runs or read it back with ReadFile\n   - If you made edits: verify changes with ReadFile\n   - If you created files: confirm they exist with List or TreeView\n   - If you deleted files: confirm they no longer exist\n5. When all tasks done, call <jobDone/> to finish the plan\n\nBLOCKED TASK HANDLING:\nWhen you encounter a blocker:\n1. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted X, blocked because Y</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n2. Call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> and explain EXACTLY:\n   - What you tried to do\n   - What blocked you (error message, missing file, etc.)\n   - What specific information or action is needed to unblock\n   - What the user should do or provide\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <Terminal><arg1>ls</arg1><arg2>-l</arg2></Terminal>: Execute terminal commands. Use ONLY for one-liner commands. Params: <arg1>, [<arg2>], ... (dynamic args)\n- <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile>: Read file. Params: <fileName>\n- <WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Simple hello world app.</contentOfFile></WriteFile>: Write file. Use for content < 4096 bytes. For larger content, use WriteFile for first chunk then AppendFile. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <AppendFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Second line</contentOfFile><fromLineNumber>1</fromLineNumber></AppendFile>: Append to file. Use for content > 4096 bytes or adding to existing files. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). If file exists and you want to overwrite, use WriteFile instead. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <List><path>.</path></List>: List files. Prefer this over Terminal ls. Params: [<path>] (optional)\n- <listTools/>: Show all tools. No params.\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView>: Show directory tree. Explore project structure, set depth=0 for unlimited. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n- <ExecuteScript><fileName>ls</fileName><args>-l</args></ExecuteScript>: Run script (.py, .sh, .js, etc). Params: <fileName>, [<args>]\n- <Grep><pattern>search_term</pattern><fileName>file.txt</fileName><recursive>true</recursive></Grep>: Search by regex. Prefer this over Terminal grep. Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\n  **CRITICAL: Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers. When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range. After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify.\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\n\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\n- <deleteTask><taskId>id</taskId></deleteTask> - Remove a task from the current plan.\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\n\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\n1. Task received: \"Create project folder with basic files\"\n2. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\n\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \"Create login form\" not \"Build entire auth system\")\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\n\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\n- Easier to track progress\n- Can resume if interrupted\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\n- Parallel work possible in future\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\n1. User says: \"I want a web app with login and dashboard\"\n2. <!-- {"role": "system", "content": "\nYou are in BUILD MODE. You are code agent. Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.\n\nMODE: BUILD (Thinking ENABLED - you can reason step by step)\n\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\n1. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.\n3. MANDATORY PROGRESS REPORTING: After completing any meaningful step, call <LogProgress><taskId>TASK_ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Specific action completed</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n4. MANDATORY SELF-VERIFICATION: Before calling <nextTask>completed</nextTask>, verify your work:\n   - If you wrote code: verify it runs or read it back with ReadFile\n   - If you made edits: verify changes with ReadFile\n   - If you created files: confirm they exist with List or TreeView\n   - If you deleted files: confirm they no longer exist\n5. When a task is verified completed, call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n6. If blocked, call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> with detailed explanation\n7. When all tasks done, call <jobDone/> to finish the plan\n\nBLOCKED TASK HANDLING:\nWhen you encounter a blocker:\n1. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted X, blocked because Y</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n2. Call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> and explain EXACTLY:\n   - What you tried to do\n   - What blocked you (error message, missing file, etc.)\n   - What specific information or action is needed to unblock\n   - What the user should do or provide\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <Terminal><arg1>ls</arg1><arg2>-l</arg2></Terminal>: Execute terminal commands. Use ONLY for one-liner commands. Params: <arg1>, [<arg2>], ... (dynamic args)\n- <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile>: Read file. Params: <fileName>\n- <WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Simple hello world app.</contentOfFile></WriteFile>: Write file. Use for content < 4096 bytes. For larger content, use WriteFile for first chunk then AppendFile. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\n- <AppendFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Second line</contentOfFile><fromLineNumber>1</fromLineNumber></AppendFile>: Append to file. Use for content > 4096 bytes or adding to existing files. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\n  **CRITICAL: Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers. When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range. After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify.\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\n\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\n- <deleteTask><taskId>id</taskId></deleteTask> - Remove a task from the current plan.\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\n\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\n1. Task received: \"Create project folder with basic files\"\n2. Use Terminal to create folder: mkdir myproject\n3. Use WriteFile/CreateFile to create index.html, style.css, app.js\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>1</taskId><whatWasDone>Created project folder with 3 files</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Read back files with ReadFile to verify content is correct\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\n7. Next task is received automatically\n8. Repeat until all tasks done\n9. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (self-created tasks in build mode):\n1. Create plan and tasks with createPlan + createTask\n2. Call <planDone/> to start the first pending task\n3. Execute the task using available tools\n4. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>What was accomplished</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. Verify work with ReadFile/List/TreeView\n6. Call <nextTask>completed</nextTask> when done\n7. Repeat until all tasks done\n8. Call <jobDone/> when finished\n\nBLOCKED EXAMPLE:\n1. Task: \"Install dependency X\"\n2. Attempt: <Terminal><arg1>pip</arg1><arg2>install</arg2><arg3>package-that-does-not-exist</arg3></Terminal>\n3. Error: \"Package not found\"\n4. <LogProgress><taskId>3</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted to install package-that-does-not-exist, failed with error: Package not found</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\n5. <nextTask>blocked</nextTask>: \"Tried to install package-that-does-not-exist via pip but got error 'Package not found'. Need to verify correct package name or install from alternative source. User should provide correct package name or installation method.\"\n", "sessionId": 204, "rowId": 1, "timestamp": 1782969646.060839, "date": "2026-07-02"} -->

For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \\u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \\u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\\\"Hello\\\"` not `\\\"Hello\\\"`).\\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\\n\\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \\u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\\\"Hello\\\"` not `\\\"Hello\\\"`).\\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. The user may provide files to read directly.\\n\\nPHASE 1 - CREATE PLAN:\\nCall <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal description</instructions></createPlan>\\n\\nPHASE 2 - CREATE TASKS:\\nCall <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed instruction for this task</instruction></createTask> for each step\\n\\nPHASE 3 - FINALIZE:\\nWhen all tasks are created, tell user: \\\"Plan is ready! Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\\\"\\n\\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\\n\\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \\\"Create login form\\\" not \\\"Build entire auth system\\\")\\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\\n\\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\\n- Easier to track progress\\n- Can resume if interrupted\\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\\n- Parallel work possible in future\\n\\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\\n\\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \\u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \\u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\\\"Hello\\\"` not `\\\"Hello\\\"`).\\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\\n\\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\\n1. User says: \\\"I want a web app with login and dashboard\\\"\\n2. MANDATORY SELF-VERIFICATION: Before calling <nextTask>completed</nextTask>, verify your work:\\n   - If you wrote code: verify it runs or read it back with ReadFile\\n   - If you made edits: verify changes with ReadFile\\n   - If you created files: confirm they exist with List or TreeView\\n   - If you deleted files: confirm they no longer exist\\n5. When a task is verified completed, call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\\n6. If blocked, call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> with detailed explanation\\n7. Use ONLY for one-liner commands. Params: <arg1>, [<arg2>], ... (dynamic args)\\n- <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile>: Read file. Params: <fileName>\\n- <WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Simple hello world app.</contentOfFile></WriteFile>: Write file. Use for content < 4096 bytes. For larger content, use WriteFile for first chunk then AppendFile. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\\n- <AppendFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Second line</contentOfFile><fromLineNumber>1</fromLineNumber></AppendFile>: Append to file. Use for content > 4096 bytes or adding to existing files. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). If file exists and you want to overwrite, use WriteFile instead. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\\n- <List><path>.</path></List>: List files. Prefer this over Terminal ls. Params: [<path>] (optional)\\n- <listTools/>: Show all tools. No params.\\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView>: Show directory tree. Explore project structure, set depth=0 for unlimited. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\\n- <ExecuteScript><fileName>ls</fileName><args>-l</args></ExecuteScript>: Run script (.py, .sh, .js, etc). Params: <fileName>, [<args>]\\n- <Grep><pattern>search_term</pattern><fileName>file.txt</fileName><recursive>true</recursive></Grep>: Search by regex. Prefer this over Terminal grep. Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\\n  **CRITICAL: Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers. When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range. After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify.\\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\\n\\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\\n- <deleteTask><taskId>id</taskId></deleteTask> - Remove a task from the current plan.\\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\\n\\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \\u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\\\"Hello\\\"` not `\\\"Hello\\\"`).\\n\\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\\n1. Task received: \\\"Create project folder with basic files\\\"\\n2. Use Terminal to create folder: mkdir myproject\\n3. Use WriteFile/CreateFile to create index.html, style.css, app.js\\n4. Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\\\\\\\\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\\\\\\\\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\\\\\\\\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\\\\\\\\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\\\\\\\\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\\\\\\\\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\\\\\\\\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Create login form\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\" not \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Build entire auth system\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\")\\\\\\\\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\\\\\\\\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\\\\\\\\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\\\\\\\\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\\\\\\\\n- Easier to track progress\\\\\\\\n- Can resume if interrupted\\\\\\\\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\\\\\\\\n- Parallel work possible in future\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\\\\\\\\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\\\\\\\\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\\\\\\\\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\\\\\\\\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\\\\\\\\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\\\\\\\\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\\\\\\\\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\\\\\\\\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\\\\\\\\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\\\\\\\\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \\\\\\\\u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\\\\\\\\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\\\\\\\\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\\\\\\\\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\\\\\\\\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\\\\\\\\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\\\\\\\\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\\\\\\\\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\\\\\\\\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\\\\\\\\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\\\\\\\\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\\\\\\\\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \\\\\\\\u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"` not `\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\"`).\\\\\\\\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\\\\\\\\n\\\\\\\\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\\\\\\\\n1. You are code agent. Your role is to execute the tasks created in plan mode.\\\\n\\\\nMODE: BUILD (Thinking ENABLED - you can reason step by step)\\\\n\\\\nIMPORTANT WORKFLOW:\\\\n1. You will receive tasks automatically (from plan mode). Execute each task using available tools.\\\\n2. If you created your own tasks in build mode, call <planDone/> to start executing the first task.\\\\n3. MANDATORY PROGRESS REPORTING: After completing any meaningful step, call <LogProgress><taskId>TASK_ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Specific action completed</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\\\\n4. MANDATORY SELF-VERIFICATION: Before calling <nextTask>completed</nextTask>, verify your work:\\\\n   - If you wrote code: verify it runs or read it back with ReadFile\\\\n   - If you made edits: verify changes with ReadFile\\\\n   - If you created files: confirm they exist with List or TreeView\\\\n   - If you deleted files: confirm they no longer exist\\\\n5. When a task is verified completed, call <nextTask>completed</nextTask>\\\\n6. If blocked, call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> with detailed explanation\\\\n7. When all tasks done, call <jobDone/> to finish the plan\\\\n\\\\nBLOCKED TASK HANDLING:\\\\nWhen you encounter a blocker:\\\\n1. Call <LogProgress><taskId>ID</taskId><whatWasDone>Attempted X, blocked because Y</whatWasDone></LogProgress>\\\\n2. Call <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> and explain EXACTLY:\\\\n   - What you tried to do\\\\n   - What blocked you (error message, missing file, etc.)\\\\n   - What specific information or action is needed to unblock\\\\n   - What the user should do or provide\\\\n\\\\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\\\\n- <Terminal><arg1>ls</arg1><arg2>-l</arg2></Terminal>: Execute terminal commands. Use ONLY for one-liner commands. Params: <arg1>, [<arg2>], ... (dynamic args)\\\\n- <ReadFile><fileName>README.md</fileName></ReadFile>: Read file. Params: <fileName>\\\\n- <WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Simple hello world app.</contentOfFile></WriteFile>: Write file. Use for content < 4096 bytes. For larger content, use WriteFile for first chunk then AppendFile. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\\\\n- <AppendFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># Second line</contentOfFile><fromLineNumber>1</fromLineNumber></AppendFile>: Append to file. Use for content > 4096 bytes or adding to existing files. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\\\\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). If file exists and you want to overwrite, use WriteFile instead. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>\\\\n- <List><path>.</path></List>: List files. Prefer this over Terminal ls. Params: [<path>] (optional)\\\\n- <listTools/>: Show all tools. No params.\\\\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView>: Show directory tree. Explore project structure, set depth=0 for unlimited. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\\\\n- <ExecuteScript><fileName>ls</fileName><args>-l</args></ExecuteScript>: Run script (.py, .sh, .js, etc). Params: <fileName>, [<args>]\\\\n- <Grep><pattern>search_term</pattern><fileName>file.txt</fileName><recursive>true</recursive></Grep>: Search by regex. Prefer this over Terminal grep. Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\\\\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\\\\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\\\\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\\\\n  **CRITICAL: Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers. When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range. After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify.\\\\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\\\\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\\\\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\\\\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\\\\n\\\\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\\\\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\\\\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\\\\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \\\\u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\\\\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\\\\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\\\\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\\\\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\\\\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\\\\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\\\\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\\\\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\\\\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\\\\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\\\\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \\\\u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\"` not `\\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\"`).\\\\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\\\\n\\\\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\\\\n1. User says: \\\\\\\"I want a web app with login and dashboard\\\\\\\"\\\\n2. Params: <fileName>, <contentOfFile>, [<fromLineNumber>]\\\\n- <CreateFile><fileName>testfile.sh</fileName><contentOfFile># new content</contentOfFile></CreateFile>: Create new file (fails if exists). Params: [<path>] (optional)\\\\n- <listTools/>: Show all tools. No params.\\\\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView>: Show directory tree. Explore project structure, set depth=0 for unlimited. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\\\\n- <ExecuteScript><fileName>ls</fileName><args>-l</args></ExecuteScript>: Run script (.py, .sh, .js, etc). Params: <fileName>, [<args>]\\\\n- <Grep><pattern>search_term</pattern><fileName>file.txt</fileName><recursive>true</recursive></Grep>: Search by regex. Prefer this over Terminal grep. Params: <pattern>, [<fileName>], [<recursive>]\\\\n- <Diff><file1>file1.txt</file1><file2>file2.txt</file2><unified>3</unified></Diff>: Compare files. Params: <file1>, <file2>, [<unified>]\\\\n- <Sed><pattern>old_text</pattern><replacement>new_text</replacement><fileName>file.txt</fileName><inplace>true</inplace></Sed>: Find/replace. Params: <pattern>, <replacement>, <fileName>, [<inplace>]\\\\n- <ReplaceLine><fileName>file.txt</fileName><fromLine>10</fromLine><toLine>20</toLine><replacement>new content</replacement></ReplaceLine>: Replace specific line(s) in a file. Use for targeted edits instead of rewriting the whole file. Params: <fileName>, <fromLine> (required), [<toLine>] (optional, defaults to fromLine), <replacement>\\\\n  **CRITICAL: Always ReadFile first to get correct line numbers. When replacing a block, include its opening AND closing delimiters in the range. After ReplaceLine, ReadFile to verify.\\\\n- <Find><pattern>*.py</pattern><path>.</path></Find>: Find by name. Prefer this over Terminal find. Params: <pattern>, [<path>]\\\\n- <Head><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Head>: First N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\\\\n- <Tail><fileName>file.txt</fileName><lines>10</lines></Tail>: Last N lines. Params: <fileName>, [<lines>]\\\\n- <Sort><fileName>file.txt</fileName><numeric>true</numeric></Sort>: Sort lines. Params: <fileName>, [<numeric>], [<reverse>], [<unique>]\\\\n\\\\nPLAN MANAGEMENT TOOLS (use these to track progress):\\\\n- <planDone/> - Signal planning is done, start the first pending task\\\\n- <nextTask>completed</nextTask> - Mark current task completed, get next task\\\\n- <nextTask>blocked</nextTask> - Mark current task blocked, explain why\\\\n- <LogProgress><taskId>task_id</taskId><whatWasDone>What you did</whatWasDone></LogProgress> - Log progress on current task\\\\n- <viewTask/> - View current plan and tasks\\\\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks\\\\n- <jobDone/> - Finish the plan (only when all tasks are done or you want to end early)\\\\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>Goal description</instructions></createPlan> - Create a new plan (replaces current). Use when current plan needs full replacement.\\\\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>What to do</instruction></createTask> - Add a new task to the current plan. Always create a plan first.\\\\n- <updateTask><taskId>id</taskId><title>New Title</title><instruction>New instruction</instruction></updateTask> - Update a task's title and/or instruction.\\\\n- <deleteTask><taskId>id</taskId></deleteTask> - Remove a task from the current plan.\\\\n- <deletePlan/> - Delete the current plan entirely.\\\\n- <deleteDraft/> - Delete the unsaved draft plan.\\\\n- <deleteAllPlans/> - Delete all plans.\\\\n\\\\nTOOL USAGE RULES:\\\\n- NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\\\\n- Prefer targeted edits: Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. This is more precise and preserves unrelated content.\\\\n- Prefer XML tools (Grep, Find, List) over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\\\\n- For file manipulation with complex data, use WriteFile/AppendFile. For one-liners, echo/cat/tee with Terminal is fine.\\\\n- Use ExecuteScript to run scripts you create (WriteFile/CreateFile). Terminal is for system binaries only.\\\\n- Save useful commands and solutions as tips with <SaveTip>. Retrieve them with <GetTip>. Browse with <ListTips>. Bring saved tips into context with <ReinsertTip>.\\\\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \\\\u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\"` not `\\\\\\\"Hello\\\\\\\"`).\\\\n\\\\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW (tasks from plan mode):\\\\n1. \"\"\"Base command class\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, db: Database):\n        self.db = db\n    \n    def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Execute the command with True\n\n\nclass CreateTableCommand(Command):\n    \"\"\"CREATE TABLE command\"\"\"\n    \n    def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name required\"\n        \n        table_name = params['table']\n        try:\n            self.db.create_table(table_name)\n            return f\"OK:         return \"ERROR: No valid data to insert\"\n        \n        try:\n            # Use first key as record key, rest as value\n            keys = list(data.keys())\n            if not keys:\n                return \"ERROR: Empty data\"\n            \n            record_key = keys[0]\n            record_value = str(data)\n            \n            self.db.insert(table_name, record_key, record_value)\n            return f\"OK: Inserted into '{table_name}' with key '{record_key}'\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {str(e)}\"\n\n\nclass SelectCommand(Command):\n    \"\"\"SELECT command\"\"\"\n    \n    def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name required\"\n        \n        table_name = params['table']\n        key = params.get('key')\n        \n        try:\n            results = self.db.select(table_name, key)\n {v}\" for k, v in results.items()]\n                return \"OK:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join(lines)\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {str(e)}\"\n\n\nclass UpdateCommand(Command):\n    \"\"\"UPDATE command\"\"\"\n    \n    def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table', 'data']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name and data required\"\n        \n        table_name = params['table']\n        key = params.get('key')\n        data = params.get('parsed_data', {})\n        \n        if not key:\n            return \"ERROR: Key required for UPDATE\"\n        \n        try:\n            record_value = str(data)\n            self.db.update(table_name, key, record_value)\n            return \"\"\"SHOW TABLES command\"\"\"\n    \n    def execute(self, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:\n        # This is a placeholder - LevelDB doesn't have a native list tables\n        # In a real INSERT INTO <table> VALUES key=value,key2=value2\n                               - Insert a record\n  SELECT * FROM <table>        - Select all records\n  SELECT * FROM <table> WHERE key=<key>\n                               - Select specific record\n  UPDATE <table> SET key=value WHERE key=<key>\n                               - Update a record\n  DELETE FROM <table> WHERE key=<key>\n UpdateCommand(db),\n            'DELETE': DeleteCommand(db),\n            'SHOW': ShowTablesCommand(db),\n            'HELP': HelpCommand(db),\n        }\n    \n    def execute(self, command_type: self.users = {\n            'admin': self._hash_password('skrlat')\n        }\n        self.active_sessions: Set[str] = set()\n    \n    def _hash_password(self, password: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Hash a password using SHA-256\"\"\"\n        return hashlib.sha256(password.encode()).hexdigest()\n    \n    def authenticate(self, username: str, password: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Verify username and password\"\"\"\n        if username not in self.users:\n            return False\n        password_hash = self._hash_password(password)\n        return self.users[username] == password_hash\n    \n    def create_session(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create a new session token\"\"\"\n        token = secrets.token_hex(16)\n        self.active_sessions.add(token)\n        return token\n    \n    def validate_session(self, token: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if session token is valid\"\"\"\n        return token in self.active_sessions\n    \n    def self.send(\"Login required. Format: USER <username>\")\n            \n            while self.running:\n                # Receive command\n                data = self.receive()\n                if data is None:\n                    break\n                \n                print(f\"[SERVER] Received from {self.address}: {data}\")\n                \n                # Handle authentication\n                if not self.authenticated:\n                    response = self._handle_auth(data)\n                    self.send(response)\n                    if response.startswith(\"ERROR\") or response == \"BYE\":\n                        break\n                    continue\n                \n                # Handle commands\n                if data.upper() in ('QUIT', 'EXIT'):\n                    self.send(\"BYE\")\n                    break\n                \n                # Parse and execute command\n                cmd_type, params = self.parser.parse(data)\n                \n                # Type HELP for commands.\"\n            else:\n                return \"ERROR: Invalid credentials\"\n        \n        elif command in ('QUIT', 'EXIT'):\n            return \"BYE\"\n        \n        else:\n            return \"ERROR: Authentication required. Use USER <username>\"\n\n\nclass SocketServer:\n    \"\"\"Threaded TCP Socket Server\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, host: str = '0.0.0.0', port: int = 9999, \n                 db_path: str = socket.SOCK_STREAM)\\n        self.socket.connect((self.host, self.port))\\n        return self\\n    \\n    def send(self, message):\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Send message\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        self.socket.sendall(message.encode() + b'\\\\n')\\n    \\n    def receive(self):\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Receive message\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        data = self.socket.recv(4096)\\n        return data.decode().strip() if data else None\\n    \\n    def close(self):\\n        \\\"\\\"\\\"Close connection\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n        if self.socket:\\n            self.socket.close()\\n    \\n    def <!-- {"role": "system", "content": "\nYou are in PLAN MODE. You are architect. Type !MODE build to start BUILD mode.\"\n\nHOW TO SPLIT USER INSTRUCTIONS INTO TASKS:\n1. Analyze the user's goal - what is the end result they want?\n2. Identify distinct steps that can be done independently\n3. Create tasks for each step with clear, actionable instructions\n4. Order matters - earlier tasks should enable later ones\n5. Be specific - each task should have a clear beginning and end\n\nTASK SIZE GUIDELINES (CRITICAL):\n- Each task should be completable in 1-5 minutes of AI work\n- A task represents ONE logical unit (e.g., \"Create login form\" not \"Build entire auth system\")\n- If a task requires >3 file edits, split it into smaller tasks\n- Tasks should be independently verifiable\n- Prefer 5-10 small tasks over 1-2 large ones\n- Each task should have clear success criteria\n\nWHY SPLIT INTO TASKS:\n- Easier to track progress\n- Can resume if interrupted\n- Better error handling (failure of one task doesn't affect others)\n- Parallel work possible in future\n\nAVAILABLE TOOLS (use exact XML format):\n- <createPlan><title>Plan Title</title><instructions>High-level goal and context</instructions></createPlan> - Create the plan FIRST\n- <createTask><title>Task Title</title><instruction>Detailed step-by-step instruction for the model to follow when executing this task</instruction></createTask> - Add tasks AFTER creating plan\n- <updateTask><id>taskId</id><status>pending|completed|blocked</status></updateTask> - Update task status\n- <deleteTask><id>taskId</id></deleteTask> - Remove a task\n- <viewTask/> or <viewTask><id>taskId</id></viewTask> - View plan or specific task\n- <listTasks/> - List all tasks in current plan\n- <TreeView><path>.</path><depth>3</depth></TreeView> - Show directory tree. Params: [<path>], [<depth>] (default 3), [<pattern>] (glob filter), [<showHidden>]\n\nTOOL USAGE GUIDELINES:\n- Terminal: Use ONLY for one-liner commands. For complex scripts or data processing, use WriteFile/CreateFile.\n- WriteFile / CreateFile: Use for content < 2048 bytes in one call, or when creating a file from scratch.\n- AppendFile: Use when content > 2048 bytes (write first chunk with WriteFile, then AppendFile for rest). Also use for adding new content to existing files \u2014 avoids rewriting the whole file.\n- ReplaceLine: Use for targeted line edits. Specify a single line or a range of lines to replace with new content. Prefer this over WriteFile when you only need to change specific lines.\n  **CRITICAL ReplaceLine rules:**\n  - Always ReadFile first to count lines and get exact line numbers (1-indexed)\n  - When replacing a block (CSS rule, function, class), include BOTH the opening AND closing delimiters in the range\n  - Example: to replace a block on lines 15-22, set fromLine=15, toLine=22\n  - After ReplaceLine, use ReadFile to verify the result looks correct\n  - If unsure about line range, replace fewer lines and iterate\n- TreeView: Use to explore project directory structure. Set depth=0 for unlimited depth.\n- General Rule: NEVER call multiple tool calls for large content. Split large data: WriteFile first chunk -> AppendFile remaining.\n- Grep / Find / List / TreeView: Prefer these XML tools over Terminal commands (grep, find, ls).\n- XML Content: Never use backslashes to escape characters inside XML values \u2014 the parser handles special characters natively. Write raw content without escaping quotes (write `\"Hello\"` not `\"Hello\"`).\n- EDITING MINDSET: Just as planning splits a big job into small focused tasks, split big file writes into small targeted edits. Use ReplaceLine for specific line changes and AppendFile for additions instead of rewriting entire files with WriteFile. Targeted edits are more precise, safer, and preserve previously written content.\n\nEXAMPLE WORKFLOW:\n1. User says: \"I want a web app with login and dashboard\"\n2. <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nTest client for threaded socket server with LevelDB backend.\nTests authentication and SQL-like commands.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport socket\nimport sys\nimport time\n\nHOST = 'localhost'\nPORT = 9999\n\n\ndef send_command(sock, command):\n    \"\"\"Send a command and receive response.\"\"\"\n    sock.sendall((command + '\\n').encode())\n    response = sock.recv(4096).decode().strip()\n    return response\n\n\ndef test_authentication():\n    \"\"\"Test authentication flow.\"\"\"\n    print(\"=\" * 50)\n    print(\"TEST: Authentication\")\n    print(\"=\" * 50)\n    \n    with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as sock:\n        sock.connect((HOST, PORT))\n        \n        # <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "I see the issue! Several files are missing. Let me create them:   </think>  <WriteFile><fileName>parser.py</fileName><contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nSQL-like Command Parser for LevelDB Socket Server\nParses MySQL-like commands into structured operations\n\"\"\"\n\nimport re\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, Optional, Tuple\n\n\nclass CommandParser:\n    \"\"\"Parse SQL-like commands for LevelDB operations\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.patterns = {\n            'CREATE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*CREATE\\s+TABLE\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)(?:\\s*\\((?P<columns>[^)]+)\\))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'DROP': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*DROP\\s+TABLE\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'INSERT': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*INSERT\\s+INTO\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)\\s+VALUES\\s*\\((?P<values>[^)]+)\\)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SELECT': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SELECT\\s+(?P<columns>[\\w\\s*,]+)\\s+FROM\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)(?:\\s+WHERE\\s+(?P<where>.+))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'UPDATE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*UPDATE\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)\\s+SET\\s+(?P<set>.+?)(?:\\s+WHERE\\s+(?P<where>.+))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'DELETE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*DELETE\\s+FROM\\s+(?P<table>\\w+)(?:\\s+WHERE\\s+(?P<where>.+))?\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'USE': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*USE\\s+(?P<database>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'CREATE_DB': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*CREATE\\s+DATABASE\\s+(?P<database>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'DROP_DB': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*DROP\\s+DATABASE\\s+(?P<database>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_TABLES': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+TABLES\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'HELP': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*HELP\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'QUIT': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*(?:QUIT|EXIT)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n        }\n    \n    def parse(self, command: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[Dict[str, Any]]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Parse a command string into (command_type, parameters)\n        \n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (command_type, params_dict) or ('UNKNOWN', None) if not recognized\n        \"\"\"\n        command = command.strip()\n        \n        # Check for special commands first\n        if command.upper() == 'HELP':\n            return 'HELP', {}\n        if command.upper() in ('QUIT', 'EXIT'):\n            return 'QUIT', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'SHOW TABLES':\n            return 'SHOW_TABLES', {}\n        \n        # Try to match patterns\n        for cmd_type, pattern in self.patterns.items():\n            match = pattern.match(command)\n            if match:\n                params = match.groupdict()\n                \n                # Parse columns if present\n                if 'columns' in params and params['columns']:\n                    params['columns'] = [c.strip() for c in params['columns'].split(',')]\n                \n                # Parse values if present\n                if 'values' in params and params['values']:\n                    params['values'] = self._parse_values(params['values'])\n                \n                # Parse SET clause for UPDATE\n                if 'set' in params and params['set']:\n                    params['set'] = self._parse_set_clause(params['set'])\n                \n                # Parse WHERE clause\n                if 'where' in params and params['where']:\n                    params['where'] = self._parse_where_clause(params['where'])\n                \n                return cmd_type, params\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN', None\n    \n    def _parse_values(self, values_str: str) -> list:\n        \"\"\"Parse VALUES clause into list of values\"\"\"\n        values = []\n        current = ''\n        in_string = False\n        string_char = None\n        \n        for char in values_str:\n            if char in (\"'\", '\"') and not in_string:\n                in_string = True\n                string_char = char\n                continue\n            elif char == string_char and in_string:\n                in_string = False\n                string_char = None\n                values.append(current.strip())\n                current = ''\n                continue\n            \n            if char == ',' and not in_string:\n                if current.strip():\n                    values.append(current.strip())\n                current = ''\n            else:\n                current += char\n        \n        if current.strip():\n            values.append(current.strip())\n        \n        # Convert numeric strings to numbers\n        result = []\n        for v in values:\n            v = v.strip()\n            try:\n                if '.' in v:\n                    result.append(float(v))\n                else:\n                    result.append(int(v))\n            except ValueError:\n                result.append(v)\n        \n         col = col.strip()\n                val = val.strip()\n                \n                # Try to convert to number\n                try:\n                    if '.' in val:\n <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile><fileName>server.py</fileName><contentOfFile>#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nLevelDB Socket Server - Main Entry Point\nA threaded socket server providing MySQL-like interface over LevelDB\n\"\"\"\n\nimport socket\nimport threading\nimport sys\nimport os\n\n# Add src to path\nsys.path.insert(0, os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))\n\nfrom database import Database\nfrom auth import Authenticator\nfrom parser import CommandParser\nfrom commands import CommandRegistry\n\n\nclass ClientHandler(threading.Thread):\n    \"\"\"Handle individual client connections\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, client_socket, address, db, authenticator):\n        super().__init__(daemon=True)\n        self.client_socket = client_socket\n        self.address = address\n        self.db = db\n        self.authenticator = authenticator\n        self.parser = CommandParser()\n        self.commands = CommandRegistry(db)\n        self.authenticated = False\n        self.username = None\n        self.client_state = {\n            'current_db': None\n        }\n        self.running = True\n    \n    def send(self, message):\n        \"\"\"Send message to client\"\"\"\n        self.client_socket.sendall(message.encode() + b'\\n')\n    \n    def receive(self):\n        \"\"\"Receive message from client\"\"\"\n        data = self.client_socket.recv(4096)\n        if not data:\n            return None\n        return data.decode().strip()\n    \n    def run(self):\n        \"\"\"Main client handling loop\"\"\"\n        print(f\"[SERVER] Client connected from {self.address}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Send welcome message\n            self.send(\"=\" * 50)\n            self.send(\"LevelDB Socket Server\")\n            self.send(\"=\" * 50)\n            self.send(\"Authentication required\")\n            self.send(\"Format: USER <username>, then PASS <password>\")\n            self.send(\"-\" * 50)\n            \n            while self.running:\n                # Receive command\n                data = self.receive()\n                if data is None:\n                    break\n                \n                print(f\"[SERVER] {self.address} -> {data}\")\n                \n                # Handle authentication\n                if not self.authenticated:\n                    response = self._handle_auth(data)\n                    self.send(response)\n                    if response.startswith(\"ERROR\") or response == \"BYE\":\n                        break\n                    continue\n                \n                # Parse and execute command\n                cmd_type, params = self.parser.parse(data)\n                response = self.commands.execute(cmd_type, params, self.client_state)\n                self.send(response)\n                \n                if response == \"BYE\":\n                    break\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[SERVER] Error handling client {self.address}: {e}\")\n        \n        finally:\n            self.client_socket.close()\n            print(f\"[SERVER] Client {self.address} disconnected\")\n    \n    def _handle_auth(self, data):\n        \"\"\"Handle authentication flow\"\"\"\n        parts = data.split(None, 1)\n        \n        if not parts:\n            return \"ERROR: Invalid input\"\n        \n        command = parts[0].upper()\n        \n        if command == \"USER\":\n            if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Username required\"\n            self.username = parts[1].strip()\n            return \"OK: Username received. Send PASS <password>\"\n        \n        elif command == \"PASS\":\n            if len(parts) < 2:\n                return \"ERROR: Password required\"\n            if not self.username:\n                return \"ERROR: USER required first\"\n            \n            password = parts[1].strip()\n            if self.authenticator.authenticate(self.username, password):\n                self.authenticated = True\n                return f\"OK: Welcome {self.username}. Authentication successful.\"\n            else:\n                return \"ERROR: Authentication failed\"\n        \n        elif command in ('QUIT', 'EXIT'):\n            return \"BYE\"\n        \n        else:\n            return \"ERROR: Authentication required. Use USER <username>\"\n\n\nclass SocketServer:\n    \"\"\"Threaded TCP Socket Server\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, host='0.0.0.0', port=9999, db_path='./data.db'):\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        self.db = Database(db_path)\n        self.authenticator = Authenticator()\n        self.server_socket = None\n        self.running = False\n    \n    def start(self):\n        \"\"\"Start the server\"\"\"\n        self.server_socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n        self.server_socket.setsockopt(socket.SOL_SOCKET, socket.SO_REUSEADDR, 1)\n        self.server_socket.bind((self.host, self.port))\n        self.server_socket.listen(5)\n        self.running = True\n        \n        print(f\"[SERVER] Started on {self.host}:{self.port}\")\n        print(f\"[SERVER] Database: {self.db.db_path}\")\n        print(f\"[SERVER] Waiting for connections...\")\n        print(f\"[SERVER] Press Ctrl+C to stop\")\n        \n        try:\n            while self.running:\n                client_socket, address = self.server_socket.accept()\n                handler = ClientHandler(\n                    client_socket, address, self.db, self.authenticator\n                )\n                handler.start()\n        \n        except KeyboardInterrupt:\n            print(\"\\n[SERVER] Shutting down...\")\n        \n        finally:\n > 
> A threaded Python socket server providing a MySQL-like command interface over LevelDB backend.
> 
> ## Features
> 
> - **Threaded TCP Socket Server** - Handles multiple concurrent clients
> - **Authentication** - Simple username/password (admin/skrlat)
> - **LevelDB Backend** - Persistent key-value storage with table namespacing
> - **SQL-like Commands** - CREATE, DROP, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE
> - **Netcat Compatible** - Tes...

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile><fileName>README.md</fileName><contentOfFile># LevelDB Socket Server\n\nA threaded Python socket server providing a MySQL-like command interface over LevelDB backend.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Threaded TCP Socket Server** - Handles multiple concurrent clients\n- **Authentication** - Simple username/password (admin/skrlat)\n- **LevelDB Backend** - Persistent key-value storage with table namespacing\n- **SQL-like Commands** - CREATE, DROP, INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE\n- **Netcat Compatible** - Test with standard netcat client\n\n## Installation\n\n```bash\npip install -r requirements.txt\n```\n\n## Usage\n\n### Start the Server\n\n```bash\npython server.py\n```\n\nServer will start on port 9999 with default settings.\n\n### Connect with Netcat\n\n```bash\nnc localhost 9999\n```\n\n### Authentication\n\n```\nWelcome to LevelDB Socket Server\nAuthentication required\nFormat: USER <username>, then PASS <password>\n--------------------------------------------------\n\nUSER admin\nPASS skrlat\n```\n\n### Available Commands\n\n| Command | Description |\n|---------|-------------|\n| `CREATE DATABASE <name>` | Create a new database |\n| `DROP DATABASE <name>` | Delete a database |\n| `USE <database>` | Select database to use |\n| `CREATE TABLE <name> (cols...)` | Create a new table |\n| `DROP TABLE <name>` | Delete a table |\n| `INSERT INTO <table> VALUES (val...)` | Insert a record |\n| `SELECT * FROM <table>` | Select all records |\n| `SELECT col FROM <table> WHERE cond` | Select specific records |\n| `UPDATE <table> SET col=val WHERE...` | Update records |\n| `DELETE FROM <table> WHERE cond` | Delete records |\n| `SHOW TABLES` | List tables |\n| `HELP` | Show help |\n| `QUIT` / `EXIT` | Disconnect |\n\n### Example Session\n\n```\n> CREATE DATABASE testdb\nOK: Database 'testdb' created\n\n> USE testdb\nOK: Using database 'testdb'\n\n> CREATE TABLE users (id INT, name TEXT)\nOK: Table 'users' created\n\n> INSERT INTO users VALUES (1, 'John')\nOK: Inserted into 'users'\n\n> INSERT INTO users VALUES (2, 'Jane')\nOK: Inserted into 'users'\n\n> SELECT * FROM
